2/17/22, 8:16 PM - Anjali: What's the problem?
One of the primary causes of hunger across the world is widespread poverty. Markets are not easily accessible and often have limited availability causes a lack of access to food. The lack of money makes it so that many cannot get enough of the nutritious food they need. 

Second cause of hunger is that many foods are being wasted, the remaining food of the night in many restaurants or functions is thrown away daily as stale. It is the story of almost every developed and developing country.

we are ranked 67 in the World Hunger.
every fourth person in India is forced to sleep with hunger. Of course, looking at the data many times is a cause for concern, but we are not ready to let go of our carelessness.
2/17/22, 8:16 PM - Anjali: The Idea
The biggest question is how can we reduce ‘food waste’ on a personal level? 
So here we come with an Idea and developed an application named as FEEDI and it is food donation platform that helps in minimizing food wastage and to utilise the left over food by redistributing extra food to people in need and feeding people with untouched nutritious.
FEEDI acts a bridge between provider that will be restaurants , party or functions organizers etc and consumer that will be NGO's 
In this platform provider will be able to share their edibles items and consumer can have access to those. 
Through FEEDI providers not only make difference in good wastage system but they will also be the part of donation
